â”‚    10 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚

â”‚    16 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    17 +  Some RMS export headers contain spaces; the "standard" name is what we                                                                â”‚

â”‚    23 +  | `Incident Time` | `IncidentTime` | Temporal |                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚    24 +  | `Incident Date_Between` | `IncidentDateBetween` | Temporal |                                                                        â”‚

â”‚    27 +  | `Report Time` | `ReportTime` | Temporal |                                                                                           â”‚

â”‚    29 +  | `Incident Type_2` | `IncidentType2` | Incident Classification |                                                                     â”‚
â”‚    30 +  | `Incident Type_3` | `IncidentType3` | Incident Classification |                                                                     â”‚
â”‚    31 +  | `FullAddress` | `FullAddress` | Location |                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚    32 +  | `Grid` | `Grid` | Location |                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    33 +  | `Zone` | `Zone` | Location |                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    34 +  | `Narrative` | `Narrative` | Incident Details |                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚    35 +  | `Total Value Stolen` | `TotalValueStolen` | Property |                                                                              â”‚
â”‚    36 +  | `Total Value Recover` | `TotalValueRecover` | Property |                                                                            â”‚
â”‚    37 +  | `Registration 1` | `Registration1` | Vehicle |                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚    38 +  | `Make1` | `Make1` | Vehicle |                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚    39 +  | `Model1` | `Model1` | Vehicle |                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚    40 +  | `Reg State 1` | `RegState1` | Vehicle |                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚    41 +  | `Registration 2` | `Registration2` | Vehicle |                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚    42 +  | `Reg State 2` | `RegState2` | Vehicle |                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚    43 +  | `Make2` | `Make2` | Vehicle |                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚    44 +  | `Model2` | `Model2` | Vehicle |                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚    45 +  | `Reviewed By` | `ReviewedBy` | Case Management |                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚    46 +  | `CompleteCalc` | `CompleteCalc` | Case Management |                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚    47 +  | `Officer of Record` | `OfficerOfRecord` | Personnel |                                                                               â”‚

â”‚    55 +  ## Field Definitions by Group                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    56 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    57 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚    58 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    59 +  ## ðŸ”– Incident Identification                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    60 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    61 +  ### CaseNumber                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    62 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    63 +  **Export Header**: `Case Number`                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚    64 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    65 +  - **Definition**: RMS case identifier serving as the primary key and                                                                  â”‚
â”‚       + primary join key to CAD `ReportNumberNew`.                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚    66 +  - **Source Field**: `Case Number` (RMS export)                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    67 +  - **Format**: `YY-NNNNNN` with optional supplemental suffix letter                                                                    â”‚
â”‚    68 +    - **Examples**: `25-000001`, `25-000001A`, `25-000001B`                                                                             â”‚
â”‚    69 +    - **Regex**: `^\d{2}-\d{6}([A-Z])?$`                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚    70 +  - **Logic**:                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚    71 +    - `YY` = last two digits of the year the case was created                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    72 +    - `NNNNNN` = sequential number starting at `000001` on January 1st                                                                  â”‚
â”‚       + each year                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚    73 +    - **Supplementals**: same base number with a suffix letter starting                                                                 â”‚
â”‚       + at `A` (then `B`, `C`, etc.)                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    74 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    75 +    - Must be non-null                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚    76 +    - Must match the regex pattern                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚    77 +    - Must be stored as text (not numeric) to preserve leading zeros                                                                    â”‚
â”‚    78 +    - Case-insensitive matching recommended (though typically uppercase)                                                                â”‚
â”‚    79 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚    80 +    - Primary join key to CAD `ReportNumberNew`                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    81 +    - Used in primary key matching strategy (confidence: 1.0)                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    82 +    - Normalized for matching: trim whitespace, collapse internal spaces,                                                               â”‚
â”‚       +  remove non-printable characters                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚    83 +  - **Group**: Incident                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚    84 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    85 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚    86 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    87 +  ## ðŸ“… Temporal Fields                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚    88 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    89 +  ### IncidentDate                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚    90 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    91 +  **Export Header**: `Incident Date`                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚    92 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    93 +  - **Definition**: Date when the incident occurred (not necessarily when                                                               â”‚
â”‚       +  it was reported).                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚    94 +  - **Source Field**: `Incident Date` (RMS export)                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚    95 +  - **Format**: Date type, exported as Excel date serial or `MM/dd/yyyy`                                                                â”‚
â”‚       + format                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚    96 +    - **Accepted Formats**:                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚    97 +      - Excel date serial number                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    98 +      - `MM/dd/yyyy`                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚    99 +      - `M/d/yyyy`                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   100 +      - ISO 8601 date (`YYYY-MM-DD`)                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   101 +  - **Logic**: User-entered or system-derived from incident details                                                                     â”‚
â”‚   102 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   103 +    - May be null (incidents without confirmed dates)                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   104 +    - If present, must be a valid date                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   105 +    - Should be â‰¤ `ReportDate` (flag if incident date is after report                                                                   â”‚
â”‚       + date)                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   106 +    - Timezone: `America/New_York` (recommended documentation standard)                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   107 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   108 +    - Used in **temporal_address_match** strategy (weight: 0.4 for date                                                                 â”‚
â”‚       + component)                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   109 +    - Used in **officer_temporal_match** strategy (weight: 0.3 for date                                                                 â”‚
â”‚       + component)                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   110 +    - Used in **address_zone_match** strategy (weight: 0.2, optional)                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   111 +    - Can backfill CAD `TimeofCall` date component in validation                                                                        â”‚
â”‚       + workflows                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   112 +  - **Group**: Temporal                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   113 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   114 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   115 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   116 +  ### IncidentTime                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   117 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   118 +  **Export Header**: `Incident Time`                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   119 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   120 +  - **Definition**: Time when the incident occurred (not necessarily when                                                               â”‚
â”‚       +  it was reported).                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚   121 +  - **Source Field**: `Incident Time` (RMS export)                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   122 +  - **Format**: Time type, exported as Excel time serial or `HH:mm`                                                                     â”‚
â”‚       + format                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   123 +    - **Accepted Formats**:                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   124 +      - Excel time serial number                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   125 +      - `HH:mm`                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚   126 +      - `H:mm`                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚   127 +      - `HH:mm:ss`                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   128 +  - **Logic**: User-entered or system-derived from incident details                                                                     â”‚
â”‚   129 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   130 +    - May be null                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   131 +    - If present, must be a valid time-of-day (00:00 to 23:59)                                                                          â”‚
â”‚   132 +    - Timezone: `America/New_York` (recommended documentation standard)                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   133 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   134 +    - Used in **temporal_address_match** strategy (weight: 0.3 with                                                                     â”‚
â”‚       + 1-hour tolerance)                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   135 +    - Used in **officer_temporal_match** strategy (weight: 0.2 with                                                                     â”‚
â”‚       + 2-hour tolerance)                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   136 +    - Combined with `IncidentDate` for temporal matching to CAD                                                                         â”‚
â”‚       + `TimeofCall`                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚   137 +  - **Group**: Temporal                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   138 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   139 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   140 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   141 +  ### IncidentDateBetween                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   142 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   143 +  **Export Header**: `Incident Date_Between`                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚   144 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   145 +  - **Definition**: End date of a date range for incidents occurring                                                                    â”‚
â”‚       + "between" two dates.                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   146 +  - **Source Field**: `Incident Date_Between` (RMS export)                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   147 +  - **Format**: Date type (same formats as `IncidentDate`)                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   148 +  - **Logic**: User-entered for date range incidents (e.g., theft                                                                       â”‚
â”‚       + discovered between two dates)                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚   149 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   150 +    - May be null (most incidents are point-in-time)                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   151 +    - If present, should be â‰¥ `IncidentDate`                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚   152 +    - Flag if date range exceeds reasonable threshold (e.g., > 30 days                                                                  â”‚
â”‚       + without justification)                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   153 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   154 +    - Not currently used in multi-column matching strategies                                                                            â”‚
â”‚   155 +    - Useful for incident analysis and reporting                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   156 +  - **Group**: Temporal                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   157 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   158 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   159 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   160 +  ### IncidentTimeBetween                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   161 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   162 +  **Export Header**: `Incident Time_Between`                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚   163 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   164 +  - **Definition**: End time of a time range for incidents occurring                                                                    â”‚
â”‚       + "between" two times.                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   165 +  - **Source Field**: `Incident Time_Between` (RMS export)                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   166 +  - **Format**: Time type (same formats as `IncidentTime`)                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   167 +  - **Logic**: User-entered for time range incidents                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   168 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   169 +    - May be null (most incidents are point-in-time)                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   170 +    - If present and `IncidentDateBetween` matches `IncidentDate`, should                                                               â”‚
â”‚       +  be â‰¥ `IncidentTime`                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   171 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   172 +    - Not currently used in multi-column matching strategies                                                                            â”‚
â”‚   173 +    - Useful for incident analysis and reporting                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   174 +  - **Group**: Temporal                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   175 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   176 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   177 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   178 +  ### ReportDate                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   179 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   180 +  **Export Header**: `Report Date`                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   181 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   182 +  - **Definition**: Date when the report was filed/created in RMS.                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   183 +  - **Source Field**: `Report Date` (RMS export)                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   184 +  - **Format**: Date type (same formats as `IncidentDate`)                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   185 +  - **Logic**: System-generated timestamp when report is created                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   186 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   187 +    - May be null (rare)                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚   188 +    - If both present, should be â‰¥ `IncidentDate`                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   189 +    - Flag if report date precedes incident date by unreasonable                                                                        â”‚
â”‚       + threshold (e.g., > 30 days)                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚   190 +    - Timezone: `America/New_York` (recommended documentation standard)                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   191 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   192 +    - Used for data quality validation                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   193 +    - Can help identify delayed reporting patterns                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   194 +  - **Group**: Temporal                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   195 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   196 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   197 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚

â”‚   199 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   200 +  **Export Header**: `Report Time`                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   201 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   202 +  - **Definition**: Time when the report was filed/created in RMS.                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   203 +  - **Source Field**: `Report Time` (RMS export)                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   204 +  - **Format**: Time type (same formats as `IncidentTime`)                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   205 +  - **Logic**: System-generated timestamp when report is created                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   206 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   207 +    - May be null                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   208 +    - Timezone: `America/New_York` (recommended documentation standard)                                                                 â”‚

â”‚   210 +    - Used for data quality validation                                                                                                  â”‚

â”‚   219 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   220 +  **Export Header**: `Incident Type_1`                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   221 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   222 +  - **Definition**: Primary incident type classification code or                                                                        â”‚
â”‚       + description.                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚   223 +  - **Source Field**: `Incident Type_1` (RMS export)                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   224 +  - **Format**: Text string                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   225 +    - **Examples**: `THEFT`, `ASSAULT`, `BURGLARY`, `MOTOR VEHICLE                                                                      â”‚
â”‚       + THEFT`, `VANDALISM`                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   226 +  - **Logic**: User-selected from RMS incident type dropdown/lookup                                                                     â”‚
â”‚   227 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   228 +    - May be null (though strongly recommended to populate)                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   229 +    - Should match controlled vocabulary from RMS incident type reference                                                               â”‚
â”‚       +  table                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   230 +    - Case-insensitive validation recommended                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚   231 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   232 +    - **Priority 1** for backfilling CAD `Incident` field when CAD                                                                      â”‚
â”‚       + incident is null or blank                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   233 +    - Mapped to CAD `Incident` field                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   234 +    - Backfill condition: `update_when: cad_null_or_blank`, `accept_when:                                                               â”‚
â”‚       +  rms_not_null_or_blank`                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚   235 +  - **Group**: Incident Classification                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   236 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚

â”‚   275 +  ### NIBRSClassification                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   276 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   277 +  **Export Header**: `NIBRS Classification`                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   278 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   279 +  - **Definition**: NIBRS (National Incident-Based Reporting System)                                                                    â”‚
â”‚       + classification code for the incident.                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   280 +  - **Source Field**: `NIBRS Classification` (RMS export)                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   281 +  - **Format**: Text string                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   282 +    - **Examples**: `13A - Aggravated Assault`, `23F - Theft from Motor                                                                 â”‚
â”‚       + Vehicle`, `220 - Burglary/Breaking & Entering`                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚   283 +  - **Logic**: System-derived or user-selected based on incident type and                                                               â”‚
â”‚       +  details                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   284 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   285 +    - May be null (not all incidents have NIBRS classifications)                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   286 +    - If present, should match NIBRS code structure and valid code list                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   287 +    - Recommend validation against official NIBRS code reference                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   288 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   289 +    - Used for UCR/NIBRS reporting compliance                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚   290 +    - Can be used for incident categorization in analysis workflows                                                                     â”‚
â”‚   291 +  - **Group**: Incident Classification                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   292 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚

â”‚   295 +  ## ðŸ“ Location Fields                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   296 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   297 +  ### FullAddress                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   298 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   299 +  **Export Header**: `FullAddress`                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   300 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   301 +  - **Definition**: Full incident location address string.                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   302 +  - **Source Field**: `FullAddress` (RMS export)                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   303 +  - **Format**: Text string containing comma-separated address components                                                               â”‚
â”‚   304 +    - **Example Pattern**: `123 Main Street, Hackensack, NJ 07601`                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   305 +    - **Components**: Street, City, State, ZIP                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚   306 +  - **Logic**: User-entered or geocoded from address components                                                                         â”‚
â”‚   307 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   308 +    - May be null (some incidents may not have specific addresses, e.g.,                                                                â”‚
â”‚       + city-wide alerts)                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   309 +    - If present, should contain at least one comma                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚   310 +    - Recommend validation against geocoding service or master address                                                                  â”‚
â”‚       + list                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   311 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   312 +    - Backfills CAD `FullAddress2` when CAD address is null or blank                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   313 +    - Used in **temporal_address_match** strategy (weight: 0.3, fuzzy                                                                   â”‚
â”‚       + match threshold: 0.85)                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   314 +    - Used in **address_zone_match** strategy (weight: 0.5, fuzzy match                                                                 â”‚
â”‚       + threshold: 0.90)                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   315 +    - Address normalization recommended: lowercase, remove punctuation,                                                                 â”‚
â”‚       + normalize street suffixes                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   316 +  - **Group**: Location                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   317 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   318 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   319 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   320 +  ### Grid                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   321 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   322 +  **Export Header**: `Grid`                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   323 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   324 +  - **Definition**: CAD grid / map grid identifier for the incident                                                                     â”‚
â”‚       + location.                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   325 +  - **Source Field**: `Grid` (RMS export)                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   326 +  - **Format**: Text string                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   327 +    - **Examples**: Grid codes vary by jurisdiction (to be defined from                                                                 â”‚
â”‚       + GIS/grid reference)                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   328 +  - **Logic**: System-derived from geocoded address or user-selected                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   329 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   330 +    - May be null                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   331 +    - If present, should match controlled list of known grid codes (same                                                                â”‚
â”‚       + domain as CAD `Grid`)                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   332 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   333 +    - Direct mapping to CAD `Grid` field                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚   334 +    - Backfills CAD `Grid` when CAD grid is null or blank                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   335 +  - **Group**: Location                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   336 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   337 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   338 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   339 +  ### Zone                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   340 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   341 +  **Export Header**: `Zone`                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   342 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   343 +  - **Definition**: Patrol/police zone code assigned to the incident                                                                    â”‚
â”‚       + location.                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   344 +  - **Source Field**: `Zone` (RMS export)                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   345 +  - **Format**: Integer or text (stored as string in current schema;                                                                    â”‚
â”‚       + observed as integer in analysis)                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   346 +    - **Observed Range**: `5`â€“`9` (integers only, consistent with CAD                                                                   â”‚
â”‚       + `PDZone`)                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   347 +  - **Logic**: System-derived from geocoded address or grid, or                                                                         â”‚
â”‚       + user-selected                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚   348 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   349 +    - May be null                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   350 +    - If present, must be an integer within valid zone domain (5-9)                                                                     â”‚
â”‚   351 +    - Should align with CAD `ZoneCalc`/`PDZone` domain                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   352 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   353 +    - Backfills CAD `PDZone` when CAD zone is null or blank (28.5%                                                                      â”‚
â”‚       + backfill rate observed in analysis)                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   354 +    - Used in **address_zone_match** strategy (weight: 0.3, exact match                                                                 â”‚
â”‚       + required)                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   355 +  - **Group**: Location                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   356 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   357 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   358 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   359 +  ## ðŸ“ Incident Details                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚   360 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   361 +  ### Narrative                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚   362 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   363 +  **Export Header**: `Narrative`                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   364 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   365 +  - **Definition**: Detailed narrative text describing the incident,                                                                    â”‚
â”‚       + actions taken by officers, witness statements, and case outcomes.                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   366 +  - **Source Field**: `Narrative` (RMS export)                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚   367 +  - **Format**: Long-form text (may contain multiple paragraphs,                                                                        â”‚
â”‚       + newlines, special characters)                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚   368 +    - **Example Structure**:                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚   369 +      ```                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   370 +      On [DATE] at [TIME], officers responded to [LOCATION] for a report                                                                â”‚
â”‚       + of [INCIDENT TYPE].                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   371 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   372 +      Upon arrival, officers observed [OBSERVATIONS].                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   373 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   374 +      Investigation revealed [FINDINGS].                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚   375 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   376 +      [SUSPECT/VICTIM] was identified as [DESCRIPTION].                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   377 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   378 +      [PROPERTY] was recovered/stolen with an estimated value of [VALUE].                                                               â”‚
â”‚   379 +      ```                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   380 +  - **Logic**: User-entered narrative by reporting officer                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   381 +  - **Extraction Hints**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   382 +    - **Suspect Descriptions**: Look for keywords like "suspect", "male",                                                               â”‚
â”‚       +  "female", "white", "black", "hispanic", "height", "weight", "wearing"                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   383 +    - **Vehicle Descriptions**: Look for keywords like "vehicle", "car",                                                                â”‚
â”‚       + "sedan", "SUV", "color", "make", "model", "plate", "registration"                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   384 +    - **Property Details**: Look for keywords like "stolen", "recovered",                                                               â”‚
â”‚       +  "value", "serial number", "item", "property"                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚   385 +    - **MO (Modus Operandi)**: Look for keywords describing method of                                                                   â”‚
â”‚       + operation, entry points, tools used                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   386 +    - **Times/Dates**: Look for date/time patterns (e.g., `MM/DD/YYYY`,                                                                 â”‚
â”‚       + `HH:MM`, "approximately", "between")                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   387 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   388 +    - May be null (some reports may not have narratives, though strongly                                                                â”‚
â”‚       + recommended)                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚   389 +    - If present, may contain unstructured text                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚   390 +    - Recommend checking for minimum length (e.g., > 10 characters) to                                                                  â”‚
â”‚       + ensure meaningful content                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   391 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   392 +    - Can be used for fuzzy text matching when primary keys don't match                                                                 â”‚
â”‚       + (use with caution due to unstructured nature)                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚   393 +    - Useful for extracting additional context for CAD integration (e.g.,                                                               â”‚
â”‚       +  officer actions, outcomes)                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚   394 +    - May contain information for derived fields (e.g., suspect vehicle                                                                 â”‚
â”‚       + description, property details)                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚   395 +  - **Group**: Incident Details                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚   396 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   397 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   398 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   399 +  ## ðŸ’° Property Fields                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   400 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   401 +  ### TotalValueStolen                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   402 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   403 +  **Export Header**: `Total Value Stolen`                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   404 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   405 +  - **Definition**: Total monetary value of stolen property in US                                                                       â”‚
â”‚       + dollars.                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   406 +  - **Source Field**: `Total Value Stolen` (RMS export)                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   407 +  - **Format**: Numeric (decimal)                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   408 +    - **Accepted Formats**:                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   409 +      - Numeric value (e.g., `1500.00`)                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   410 +      - Currency text with `$` and commas (e.g., `$1,500.00`)                                                                           â”‚
â”‚   411 +  - **Logic**: Sum of all stolen property item values entered in RMS                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   412 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   413 +    - May be null (not all incidents involve theft or property loss)                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   414 +    - If present, must be â‰¥ 0                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚   415 +    - Recommend flagging extremely high values (e.g., > $100,000) for                                                                   â”‚
â”‚       + manual review                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚   416 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   417 +    - Used for property crime analysis                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   418 +    - Can help identify high-value theft patterns                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   419 +  - **Group**: Property                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   420 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   421 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚

â”‚   426 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   427 +  - **Definition**: Total monetary value of recovered property in US                                                                    â”‚
â”‚       + dollars.                                                                                                                               â”‚

â”‚   578 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   579 +  - **Definition**: Primary officer assigned to the case in RMS.                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   580 +  - **Source Field**: `Officer of Record` (RMS export)                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   581 +  - **Format**: Text string                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   582 +    - **Format Variations**: May include rank, badge number, or name                                                                    â”‚
â”‚       + variations                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   583 +    - **Examples**: `Officer John Smith`, `Ofc. J. Smith`, `Smith, John                                                                 â”‚
â”‚       + (Badge 123)`                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚   584 +  - **Logic**: User-selected from officer roster or auto-populated from                                                                 â”‚
â”‚       + CAD assignment                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚   585 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   586 +    - May be null (some cases may not have assigned officers, e.g.,                                                                     â”‚
â”‚       + administrative reports)                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚   587 +    - Should match standardized officer naming convention                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   588 +    - Recommend aligning to officer standardization lookup (e.g.,                                                                       â”‚
â”‚       + `Assignment_Master_V2.csv`)                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚   589 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   590 +    - Backfills CAD `Officer` when CAD officer is null or blank                                                                         â”‚

â”‚       + normalized officer match)                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   592 +    - Officer normalization recommended: remove titles/prefixes,                                                                        â”‚
â”‚       + normalize name order, case-insensitive                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   593 +  - **Group**: Personnel                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚   594 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚

ðŸ“„ Field Format for Each Entry:

For each RMS field, output the following:

### FieldName (as markdown header)

Definition: What the field captures or represents

Source Field: Original RMS column name

Format or Regex: If applicable (e.g., dates, plates, case numbers)

Logic: If derived or calculated

Mapping Notes: Connection to CAD or matching strategies

Validation Rules: Any constraints (e.g., must not be null, belongs to a set)

Group: (e.g., Incident, Vehicle, Suspect, Location, etc.)

ðŸ“Œ Special Cases:

For fields derived from Narrative, provide:

Extraction hints (e.g., regex or keyword examples)

Whether it's optional or needs manual confirmation

Group fields logically:

Incident fields

Location fields

Victim/suspect vehicles

Person descriptions

MO (modi operandi)

Case linkage / context
