â”‚    54 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    55 +  ## Field Definitions by Group                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    56 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    57 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚    58 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    59 +  ## ðŸ”– Incident Identification                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    60 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    61 +  ### CaseNumber                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    62 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    63 +  **Export Header**: `Case Number`                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚    64 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    65 +  - **Definition**: RMS case identifier serving as the primary key and primary join key to CAD `ReportNumberNew`.                       â”‚
â”‚    66 +  - **Source Field**: `Case Number` (RMS export)                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    67 +  - **Format**: `YY-NNNNNN` with optional supplemental suffix letter                                                                    â”‚
â”‚    68 +    - **Examples**: `25-000001`, `25-000001A`, `25-000001B`                                                                             â”‚
â”‚    69 +    - **Regex**: `^\d{2}-\d{6}([A-Z])?$`                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚    70 +  - **Logic**:                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚    71 +    - `YY` = last two digits of the year the case was created                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    72 +    - `NNNNNN` = sequential number starting at `000001` on January 1st each year                                                        â”‚
â”‚    73 +    - **Supplementals**: same base number with a suffix letter starting at `A` (then `B`, `C`, etc.)                                    â”‚
â”‚    74 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    75 +    - Must be non-null                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚    76 +    - Must match the regex pattern                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚    77 +    - Must be stored as text (not numeric) to preserve leading zeros                                                                    â”‚
â”‚    78 +    - Case-insensitive matching recommended (though typically uppercase)                                                                â”‚
â”‚    79 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚    80 +    - Primary join key to CAD `ReportNumberNew`                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    81 +    - Used in primary key matching strategy (confidence: 1.0)                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    82 +    - Normalized for matching: trim whitespace, collapse internal spaces, remove non-printable characters                               â”‚
â”‚    83 +  - **Group**: Incident                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚    84 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    85 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚    86 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    87 +  ## ðŸ“… Temporal Fields                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚    88 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    89 +  ### IncidentDate                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚    90 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    91 +  **Export Header**: `Incident Date`                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚    92 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    93 +  - **Definition**: Date when the incident occurred (not necessarily when it was reported).                                             â”‚
â”‚    94 +  - **Source Field**: `Incident Date` (RMS export)                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚    95 +  - **Format**: Date type, exported as Excel date serial or `MM/dd/yyyy` format                                                         â”‚
â”‚    96 +    - **Accepted Formats**:                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚    97 +      - Excel date serial number                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    98 +      - `MM/dd/yyyy`                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚    99 +      - `M/d/yyyy`                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   100 +      - ISO 8601 date (`YYYY-MM-DD`)                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   101 +  - **Logic**: User-entered or system-derived from incident details                                                                     â”‚
â”‚   102 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   103 +    - May be null (incidents without confirmed dates)                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   104 +    - If present, must be a valid date                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   105 +    - Should be â‰¤ `ReportDate` (flag if incident date is after report date)                                                             â”‚
â”‚   106 +    - Timezone: `America/New_York` (recommended documentation standard)                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   107 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   108 +    - Used in **temporal_address_match** strategy (weight: 0.4 for date component)                                                      â”‚
â”‚   109 +    - Used in **officer_temporal_match** strategy (weight: 0.3 for date component)                                                      â”‚
â”‚   110 +    - Used in **address_zone_match** strategy (weight: 0.2, optional)                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   111 +    - Can backfill CAD `TimeofCall` date component in validation workflows                                                              â”‚
â”‚   112 +  - **Group**: Temporal                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   113 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   114 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   115 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   116 +  ### IncidentTime                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   117 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   118 +  **Export Header**: `Incident Time`                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   119 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   120 +  - **Definition**: Time when the incident occurred (not necessarily when it was reported).                                             â”‚
â”‚   121 +  - **Source Field**: `Incident Time` (RMS export)                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   122 +  - **Format**: Time type, exported as Excel time serial or `HH:mm` format                                                              â”‚
â”‚   123 +    - **Accepted Formats**:                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   124 +      - Excel time serial number                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   125 +      - `HH:mm`                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚   126 +      - `H:mm`                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚   127 +      - `HH:mm:ss`                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   128 +  - **Logic**: User-entered or system-derived from incident details                                                                     â”‚
â”‚   129 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   130 +    - May be null                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   131 +    - If present, must be a valid time-of-day (00:00 to 23:59)                                                                          â”‚
â”‚   132 +    - Timezone: `America/New_York` (recommended documentation standard)                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   133 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   134 +    - Used in **temporal_address_match** strategy (weight: 0.3 with 1-hour tolerance)                                                   â”‚
â”‚   135 +    - Used in **officer_temporal_match** strategy (weight: 0.2 with 2-hour tolerance)                                                   â”‚
â”‚   136 +    - Combined with `IncidentDate` for temporal matching to CAD `TimeofCall`                                                            â”‚
â”‚   137 +  - **Group**: Temporal                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   138 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   139 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   140 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   141 +  ### IncidentDateBetween                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   142 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   143 +  **Export Header**: `Incident Date_Between`                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚   144 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   145 +  - **Definition**: End date of a date range for incidents occurring "between" two dates.                                               â”‚
â”‚   146 +  - **Source Field**: `Incident Date_Between` (RMS export)                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   147 +  - **Format**: Date type (same formats as `IncidentDate`)                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   148 +  - **Logic**: User-entered for date range incidents (e.g., theft discovered between two dates)                                         â”‚
â”‚   149 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   150 +    - May be null (most incidents are point-in-time)                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   151 +    - If present, should be â‰¥ `IncidentDate`                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚   152 +    - Flag if date range exceeds reasonable threshold (e.g., > 30 days without justification)                                           â”‚
â”‚   153 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   154 +    - Not currently used in multi-column matching strategies                                                                            â”‚
â”‚   155 +    - Useful for incident analysis and reporting                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   156 +  - **Group**: Temporal                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   157 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   158 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚

â”‚   180 +  **Export Header**: `Report Date`                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   181 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   182 +  - **Definition**: Date when the report was filed/created in RMS.                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   183 +  - **Source Field**: `Report Date` (RMS export)                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   184 +  - **Format**: Date type (same formats as `IncidentDate`)                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   185 +  - **Logic**: System-generated timestamp when report is created                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   186 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   187 +    - May be null (rare)                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚   188 +    - If both present, should be â‰¥ `IncidentDate`                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   189 +    - Flag if report date precedes incident date by unreasonable threshold (e.g., > 30 days)                                            â”‚
â”‚   190 +    - Timezone: `America/New_York` (recommended documentation standard)                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   191 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   192 +    - Used for data quality validation                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   193 +    - Can help identify delayed reporting patterns                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   194 +  - **Group**: Temporal                                                                                                                 â”‚

â”‚   219 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚

â”‚   230 +    - Case-insensitive validation recommended                                                                                           â”‚

â”‚   233 +    - Mapped to CAD `Incident` field                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   234 +    - Backfill condition: `update_when: cad_null_or_blank`, `accept_when: rms_not_null_or_blank`                                        â”‚
â”‚   235 +  - **Group**: Incident Classification                                                                                                  â”‚

â”‚   295 +  ## ðŸ“ Location Fields                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   296 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   297 +  ### FullAddress                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   298 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   299 +  **Export Header**: `FullAddress`                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   300 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   301 +  - **Definition**: Full incident location address string.                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   302 +  - **Source Field**: `FullAddress` (RMS export)                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   303 +  - **Format**: Text string containing comma-separated address components                                                               â”‚
â”‚   304 +    - **Example Pattern**: `123 Main Street, Hackensack, NJ 07601`                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   305 +    - **Components**: Street, City, State, ZIP                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚   306 +  - **Logic**: User-entered or geocoded from address components                                                                         â”‚
â”‚   307 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   308 +    - May be null (some incidents may not have specific addresses, e.g., city-wide alerts)                                              â”‚
â”‚   309 +    - If present, should contain at least one comma                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚   310 +    - Recommend validation against geocoding service or master address list                                                             â”‚
â”‚   311 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   312 +    - Backfills CAD `FullAddress2` when CAD address is null or blank                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   313 +    - Used in **temporal_address_match** strategy (weight: 0.3, fuzzy match threshold: 0.85)                                            â”‚
â”‚   314 +    - Used in **address_zone_match** strategy (weight: 0.5, fuzzy match threshold: 0.90)                                                â”‚
â”‚   315 +    - Address normalization recommended: lowercase, remove punctuation, normalize street suffixes                                       â”‚
â”‚   316 +  - **Group**: Location                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   317 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚

â”‚   323 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   324 +  - **Definition**: CAD grid / map grid identifier for the incident location.                                                           â”‚
â”‚   325 +  - **Source Field**: `Grid` (RMS export)                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   326 +  - **Format**: Text string                                                                                                             â”‚

â”‚   328 +  - **Logic**: System-derived from geocoded address or user-selected                                                                    â”‚

â”‚   332 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚

â”‚   339 +  ### Zone                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   340 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   341 +  **Export Header**: `Zone`                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   342 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   343 +  - **Definition**: Patrol/police zone code assigned to the incident location.                                                          â”‚
â”‚   344 +  - **Source Field**: `Zone` (RMS export)                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   345 +  - **Format**: Integer or text (stored as string in current schema; observed as integer in analysis)                                   â”‚
â”‚   346 +    - **Observed Range**: `5`â€“`9` (integers only, consistent with CAD `PDZone`)                                                         â”‚
â”‚   347 +  - **Logic**: System-derived from geocoded address or grid, or user-selected                                                           â”‚
â”‚   348 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   349 +    - May be null                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   350 +    - If present, must be an integer within valid zone domain (5-9)                                                                     â”‚
â”‚   351 +    - Should align with CAD `ZoneCalc`/`PDZone` domain                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   352 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   353 +    - Backfills CAD `PDZone` when CAD zone is null or blank (28.5% backfill rate observed in analysis)                                  â”‚
â”‚   354 +    - Used in **address_zone_match** strategy (weight: 0.3, exact match required)                                                       â”‚
â”‚   355 +  - **Group**: Location                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   356 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   357 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   358 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   359 +  ## ðŸ“ Incident Details                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚   360 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   361 +  ### Narrative                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚   362 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   363 +  **Export Header**: `Narrative`                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   364 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   365 +  - **Definition**: Detailed narrative text describing the incident, actions taken by officers, witness statements, and case            â”‚
â”‚       + outcomes.                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   366 +  - **Source Field**: `Narrative` (RMS export)                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚   367 +  - **Format**: Long-form text (may contain multiple paragraphs, newlines, special characters)                                          â”‚
â”‚   368 +    - **Example Structure**:                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚   369 +      ```                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   370 +      On [DATE] at [TIME], officers responded to [LOCATION] for a report of [INCIDENT TYPE].                                            â”‚
â”‚   371 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   372 +      Upon arrival, officers observed [OBSERVATIONS].                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   373 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   374 +      Investigation revealed [FINDINGS].                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚   375 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   376 +      [SUSPECT/VICTIM] was identified as [DESCRIPTION].                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   377 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   378 +      [PROPERTY] was recovered/stolen with an estimated value of [VALUE].                                                               â”‚
â”‚   379 +      ```                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   380 +  - **Logic**: User-entered narrative by reporting officer                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   381 +  - **Extraction Hints**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   382 +    - **Suspect Descriptions**: Look for keywords like "suspect", "male", "female", "white", "black", "hispanic", "height", "weight",   â”‚
â”‚       +  "wearing"                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   383 +    - **Vehicle Descriptions**: Look for keywords like "vehicle", "car", "sedan", "SUV", "color", "make", "model", "plate",             â”‚
â”‚       + "registration"                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚   384 +    - **Property Details**: Look for keywords like "stolen", "recovered", "value", "serial number", "item", "property"                  â”‚
â”‚   385 +    - **MO (Modus Operandi)**: Look for keywords describing method of operation, entry points, tools used                               â”‚
â”‚   386 +    - **Times/Dates**: Look for date/time patterns (e.g., `MM/DD/YYYY`, `HH:MM`, "approximately", "between")                            â”‚
â”‚   387 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   388 +    - May be null (some reports may not have narratives, though strongly recommended)                                                   â”‚
â”‚   389 +    - If present, may contain unstructured text                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚   390 +    - Recommend checking for minimum length (e.g., > 10 characters) to ensure meaningful content                                        â”‚
â”‚   391 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   392 +    - Can be used for fuzzy text matching when primary keys don't match (use with caution due to unstructured nature)                   â”‚
â”‚   393 +    - Useful for extracting additional context for CAD integration (e.g., officer actions, outcomes)                                    â”‚
â”‚   394 +    - May contain information for derived fields (e.g., suspect vehicle description, property details)                                  â”‚
â”‚   395 +  - **Group**: Incident Details                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚   396 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   397 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   398 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   399 +  ## ðŸ’° Property Fields                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   400 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   401 +  ### TotalValueStolen                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   402 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   403 +  **Export Header**: `Total Value Stolen`                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   404 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   405 +  - **Definition**: Total monetary value of stolen property in US dollars.                                                              â”‚
â”‚   406 +  - **Source Field**: `Total Value Stolen` (RMS export)                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   407 +  - **Format**: Numeric (decimal)                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   408 +    - **Accepted Formats**:                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   409 +      - Numeric value (e.g., `1500.00`)                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   410 +      - Currency text with `$` and commas (e.g., `$1,500.00`)                                                                           â”‚
â”‚   411 +  - **Logic**: Sum of all stolen property item values entered in RMS                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   412 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   413 +    - May be null (not all incidents involve theft or property loss)                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   414 +    - If present, must be â‰¥ 0                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚   415 +    - Recommend flagging extremely high values (e.g., > $100,000) for manual review                                                     â”‚
â”‚   416 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   417 +    - Used for property crime analysis                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   418 +    - Can help identify high-value theft patterns                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   419 +  - **Group**: Property                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   420 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   421 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   422 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   423 +  ### TotalValueRecover                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   424 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚

â”‚   426 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚

â”‚   428 +  - **Source Field**: `Total Value Recover` (RMS export)                                                                                â”‚

â”‚   431 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚

â”‚   433 +    - If present, must be â‰¥ 0                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚   434 +    - Should be â‰¤ `TotalValueStolen` (flag if recovered exceeds stolen)                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   435 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   436 +    - Used for property recovery analysis and clearance rate calculations                                                               â”‚
â”‚   437 +  - **Group**: Property                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   438 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   439 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   440 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   441 +  ## ðŸš— Vehicle Fields                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   442 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   443 +  ### Registration1                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚   444 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   445 +  **Export Header**: `Registration 1`                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   446 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   447 +  - **Definition**: Vehicle registration/license plate number for the first vehicle involved in the incident.                           â”‚
â”‚   448 +  - **Source Field**: `Registration 1` (RMS export)                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚   449 +  - **Format**: Text string (format varies by state)                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   450 +    - **Examples**: `ABC123` (NJ), `ABC1234` (NY), `ABC-1234` (PA)                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   451 +  - **Logic**: User-entered from observation or DMV lookup                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   452 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   453 +    - May be null (not all incidents involve vehicles)                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   454 +    - Format varies by `RegState1`                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   455 +    - Recommend validation against state-specific plate format patterns                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   456 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   457 +    - Used for vehicle identification and tracking                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   458 +    - Can be matched against stolen vehicle databases                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   459 +  - **Group**: Vehicle                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   460 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   461 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   462 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚

â”‚   466 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   467 +  - **Definition**: State abbreviation for the first vehicle registration.                                                              â”‚
â”‚   468 +  - **Source Field**: `Reg State 1` (RMS export)                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   469 +  - **Format**: Two-letter US state abbreviation                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   470 +    - **Examples**: `NJ`, `NY`, `PA`, `CT`, `DE`                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   471 +  - **Logic**: User-selected from state dropdown                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   472 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   473 +    - May be null                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   474 +    - If present, should be valid US state abbreviation (50 states + DC + territories)                                                  â”‚
â”‚   475 +    - Recommend validation against official state code list                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   476 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   477 +    - Used to determine plate format validation rules for `Registration1`                                                               â”‚
â”‚   478 +  - **Group**: Vehicle                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   479 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   480 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   481 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   482 +  ### Make1                                                                                                                             â”‚

â”‚   487 +  - **Source Field**: `Make1` (RMS export)                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   488 +  - **Format**: Text string                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   489 +    - **Examples**: `Ford`, `Toyota`, `Honda`, `Chevrolet`, `BMW`, `Mercedes-Benz`                                                      â”‚

â”‚   491 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   492 +    - May be null                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   493 +    - Should match against known vehicle make list if available (e.g., NCIC vehicle make codes)                                         â”‚
â”‚   494 +    - Recommend standardizing capitalization and spelling                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   495 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   496 +    - Used for vehicle description and identification                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   497 +    - Can be used for pattern analysis (e.g., most stolen makes)                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   498 +  - **Group**: Vehicle                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   499 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚

â”‚   573 +  ## ðŸ‘® Personnel Fields                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚   574 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   575 +  ### OfficerOfRecord                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   576 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   577 +  **Export Header**: `Officer of Record`                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚   578 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   579 +  - **Definition**: Primary officer assigned to the case in RMS.                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   580 +  - **Source Field**: `Officer of Record` (RMS export)                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   581 +  - **Format**: Text string                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   582 +    - **Format Variations**: May include rank, badge number, or name variations                                                         â”‚
â”‚   583 +    - **Examples**: `Officer John Smith`, `Ofc. J. Smith`, `Smith, John (Badge 123)`                                                    â”‚
â”‚   584 +  - **Logic**: User-selected from officer roster or auto-populated from CAD assignment                                                  â”‚
â”‚   585 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   586 +    - May be null (some cases may not have assigned officers, e.g., administrative reports)                                             â”‚
â”‚   587 +    - Should match standardized officer naming convention                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   588 +    - Recommend aligning to officer standardization lookup (e.g., `Assignment_Master_V2.csv`)                                           â”‚
â”‚   589 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   590 +    - Backfills CAD `Officer` when CAD officer is null or blank                                                                         â”‚
â”‚   591 +    - Used in **officer_temporal_match** strategy (weight: 0.5, normalized officer match)                                               â”‚
â”‚   592 +    - Officer normalization recommended: remove titles/prefixes, normalize name order, case-insensitive                                 â”‚
â”‚   593 +  - **Group**: Personnel                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚   594 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   595 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   596 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚

â”‚   602 +  - **Source Field**: `Squad` (RMS export)                                                                                              â”‚

â”‚   610 +    - Used for squad-level analysis and reporting                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   611 +    - Can help identify squad-specific patterns or workload                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   612 +  - **Group**: Personnel                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚   613 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚

â”‚   637 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚

â”‚   639 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   640 +  - **Definition**: Officer or supervisor identifier who reviewed the case report.                                                      â”‚
â”‚   641 +  - **Source Field**: `Reviewed By` (RMS export)                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   642 +  - **Format**: Text string (same format as `OfficerOfRecord`)                                                                          â”‚

â”‚   644 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚

â”‚   647 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   648 +    - Used for quality assurance and approval tracking                                                                                  â”‚

â”‚   650 +  - **Group**: Case Management                                                                                                          â”‚

â”‚   654 +  ### CompleteCalc                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚   655 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   656 +  **Export Header**: `CompleteCalc`                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚   657 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   658 +  - **Definition**: Boolean flag indicating whether the case is marked as complete.                                                     â”‚
â”‚   659 +  - **Source Field**: `CompleteCalc` (RMS export)                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   660 +  - **Format**: Boolean or text                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚   661 +    - **Accepted Formats**:                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   662 +      - Boolean (`true`/`false`)                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   663 +      - Integer (`0`/`1`)                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   664 +      - Text (`Y`/`N`, `Yes`/`No`, `Complete`/`Incomplete`)                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   665 +  - **Logic**: System-calculated or user-toggled based on case completion criteria                                                      â”‚
â”‚   666 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   667 +    - May be null (defaults to incomplete)                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   668 +    - If present, must be coercible to boolean                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚   669 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   670 +    - Used for case completion tracking and reporting                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   671 +    - Helps identify incomplete or pending cases                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   672 +  - **Group**: Case Management                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚   673 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   674 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   675 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚

â”‚   682 +  - **Format**: Text string                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚   683 +    - **Expected Values** (to be confirmed from RMS reference):                                                                         â”‚
â”‚   684 +      - `Open`                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚   685 +      - `Closed`                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   686 +      - `Pending`                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   687 +      - `Under Investigation`                                                                                                           â”‚

â”‚   690 +      - `Cleared - Exceptional`                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚   691 +      - `Unfounded`                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚   692 +  - **Logic**: User-selected or system-derived based on case actions and outcomes                                                       â”‚
â”‚   693 +  - **Validation Rules**:                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   694 +    - May be null                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚   695 +    - Should match controlled vocabulary from RMS case status domain                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   696 +    - Recommend validation against official status code list                                                                            â”‚
â”‚   697 +  - **Mapping Notes**:                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   698 +    - Used for case lifecycle tracking and clearance analysis                                                                           â”‚
â”‚   699 +    - Critical for UCR/NIBRS reporting compliance                                                                                       â”‚

â”‚   703 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   704 +  ## Multi-Column Matching Strategy Usage                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚   705 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   706 +  The following table summarizes which RMS fields are used in each multi-column matching strategy:                                      â”‚
â”‚   707 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   708 +  | Strategy Name | RMS Fields Used | Confidence Threshold | Purpose |                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   709 +  |---------------|----------------|---------------------|---------|                                                                    â”‚
â”‚   710 +  | **Primary Key Match** | `CaseNumber` | 1.0 (100%) | Exact match on case number |                                                    â”‚
â”‚   711 +  | **Temporal + Address Match** | `IncidentDate`, `IncidentTime`, `FullAddress` | 0.85 (85%) | Match on date/time + location |         â”‚
â”‚   712 +  | **Officer + Temporal Match** | `OfficerOfRecord`, `IncidentDate`, `IncidentTime` | 0.80 (80%) | Match on officer + date/time |      â”‚
â”‚   713 +  | **Address + Zone Match** | `FullAddress`, `Zone`, `IncidentDate` (optional) | 0.75 (75%) | Match on location + zone |               â”‚
â”‚   714 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   715 +  **Detailed Strategy Documentation**: See `multi_column_matching_strategy.md` for implementation details, scoring formulas, and        â”‚
â”‚       + workflow guidance.                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚   716 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   717 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   718 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   719 +  ## Data Quality Validation Rules Summary                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   720 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   721 +  | Field Group | Key Validation Rules |                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚   722 +  |-------------|---------------------|                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚   723 +  | **Temporal** | Incident date â‰¤ Report date; Date ranges logical; Times within 24-hour format |                                      â”‚
â”‚   724 +  | **Location** | Addresses contain commas; Zones in valid range (5-9); Grid codes match reference |                                   â”‚
â”‚   725 +  | **Incident Classification** | Types match controlled vocabulary; NIBRS codes valid |                                                â”‚
â”‚   726 +  | **Vehicle** | State codes valid (50 states + DC); Make-model combinations logical |                                                 â”‚
â”‚   727 +  | **Property** | Values â‰¥ 0; Recovered â‰¤ Stolen |                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚   728 +  | **Personnel** | Officer names standardized; Match officer roster |                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   729 +  | **Case Management** | Status values match controlled vocabulary; Complete flag valid boolean |                                      â”‚
â”‚   730 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   731 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚   732 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   733 +  ## Open Confirmations (To Finalize v1.0)                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚   734 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚   735 +  1. **Controlled Vocabularies**: Confirm canonical allowed domains for:                                                                â”‚
â”‚   736 +     - `CaseStatus` (status values)                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚   737 +     - `IncidentType1/2/3` (incident type codes/descriptions)                                                                           â”‚

â”‚     1 +  # RMS Export â€” Field Definitions (v1.0)                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚     2 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚     3 +  **Document Version**: 1.0                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚     4 +  **Last Updated**: 2025-12-30                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚     5 +  **Purpose**: Comprehensive documentation of RMS export field definitions for CAD-RMS integration                                      â”‚
â”‚     6 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚     7 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚     8 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚     9 +  ## Overview                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    10 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    11 +  This document provides detailed definitions for all RMS export fields used in CAD data cleaning, enrichment, and integration          â”‚
â”‚       + workflows. Fields are organized by functional group and include validation rules, format specifications, and usage notes for           â”‚
â”‚       + multi-column matching strategies.                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚    12 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    13 +  ---                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚    14 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    15 +  ## Column Name Mapping (Export â†’ Standard)                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚    16 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    17 +  Some RMS export headers contain spaces; the "standard" name is what we use in mapping/schema work.                                    â”‚
â”‚    18 +                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    19 +  | Export Header | Standard Name | Group |                                                                                             â”‚

â”‚    23 +  | `Incident Time` | `IncidentTime` | Temporal |                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚    24 +  | `Incident Date_Between` | `IncidentDateBetween` | Temporal |                                                                        â”‚

â”‚    30 +  | `Incident Type_3` | `IncidentType3` | Incident Classification |                                                                     â”‚
